<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>sis<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> архаичн. <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <i><span title="множественное число" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">мн. ч.</span></i>: sistren (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> совр. англ. <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> шутл. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a>, напр. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:brethren.html>brethren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> sistren</b> — «<a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́тья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сёстры</a>»). 
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-sister-</b>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:скат.html>skat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skata</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href =
